\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{double__vector_8cc_source_l01791}01791     \textcolor{comment}{//===========================================================================}\textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{double__vector_8cc_source_l01792}01792 \textcolor{comment}{    /// Wrapper around the other split(...) function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{double__vector_8cc_source_l01793}01793 \textcolor{comment}{    /// Be careful with Vector of vectors. If the DoubleVectors are resized,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{double__vector_8cc_source_l01794}01794 \textcolor{comment}{    /// there could be reallocation of memory. If we wanted to use the function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{double__vector_8cc_source_l01795}01795 \textcolor{comment}{    /// which takes a Vector of pointers to DoubleVectors, we would either have}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{double__vector_8cc_source_l02056}02056 \textcolor{comment}{    /// Split a DoubleVector into the out DoubleVectors.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{double__vector_8cc_source_l02057}02057 \textcolor{comment}{    /// Data stays on its current processor, no data is sent between processors.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{double__vector_8cc_source_l02058}02058 \textcolor{comment}{    /// This results in our vectors which are a permutation of the in vector.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{double__vector_8cc_source_l02059}02059 \textcolor{comment}{    ///}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{double__vector_8cc_source_l02060}02060 \textcolor{comment}{    /// Let vec\_A be the in Vector, and let vec\_B and vec\_C be the out vectors.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{double__vector_8cc_source_l02061}02061 \textcolor{comment}{    /// Then the splitting of vec\_A is depicted below:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{double__vector_8cc_source_l02062}02062 \textcolor{comment}{    /// vec\_A: [a0  (on p0)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{double__vector_8cc_source_l02063}02063 \textcolor{comment}{    ///         a1] (on p0)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{double__vector_8cc_source_l02067}02067 \textcolor{comment}{    /// vec\_B: [a0] (on p0)    vec\_C: [a1] (on p0)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{double__vector_8cc_source_l02068}02068 \textcolor{comment}{    ///        [a2] (on p1)           [a3] (on p1).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{double__vector_8cc_source_l02069}02069 \textcolor{comment}{    ///}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{double__vector_8cc_source_l02070}02070 \textcolor{comment}{    /// This means that the distribution of the in vector MUST be a}}
